```javascript
// k6/load-tests/diyapp-load-test.js
/**
 * DIYAPP Evolution - Testes de Carga com k6
 * Objetivo: Validar estabilidade sob carga para 100% de autonomia
 */

import http from 'k6/http';
import { check, sleep, group } from 'k6';
import { Rate } from 'k6/metrics';

// Métricas customizadas
const errorRate = new Rate('errors');

// Configurações
export const options = {
  stages: [
    { duration: '2m', target: 50 },  // Ramp-up para 50 usuários
    { duration: '5m', target: 50 },  // Estabilidade
    { duration: '2m', target: 100 }, // Aumento para 100
    { duration: '5m', target: 100 }, // Estabilidade
    { duration: '2m', target: 0 },   // Ramp-down
  ],
  thresholds: {
    http_req_duration: ['p(95)<2000'], // 95% das requisições < 2s
    errors: ['rate<0.01'],             // Taxa de erro < 1%
    'http_req_failed': ['rate<0.01'],  // Falhas < 1%
  },
};

// Dados de teste
const BASE_URL = 'http://localhost:3000';
const API_URL = `${BASE_URL}/api`;

// Headers comuns
const headers = {
  'Content-Type': 'application/json',
};

export default function () {
  group('Fluxo Completo - Criação e Consulta de Projeto', () => {
    // 1. Acessa página inicial
    let res = http.get(BASE_URL);
    check(res, {
      'homepage loaded': (r) => r.status === 200,
      'homepage fast': (r) => r.timings.duration < 1000,
    }) || errorRate.add(1);

    sleep(1);

    // 2. Lista projetos
    res = http.get(`${API_URL}/projects?limit=10`);
    check(res, {
      'list projects success': (r) => r.status === 200,
      'has projects array': (r) => JSON.parse(r.body).projects.length >= 0,
    }) || errorRate.add(1);

    sleep(0.5);

    // 3. Cria novo projeto
    const projectId = __ITER % 1000; // ID único por iteração
    const projectData = JSON.stringify({
      title: `Projeto Teste ${projectId}`,
      description: `Descrição do projeto de teste ${projectId}`,
      category: 'Marcenaria',
      difficulty: 'Intermediário',
      estimatedTime: 120,
    });

    res = http.post(`${API_URL}/projects`, projectData, { headers });
    const createSuccess = check(res, {
      'create project success': (r) => r.status === 201,
      'project has id': (r) => JSON.parse(r.body).id !== undefined,
    });

    if (!createSuccess) {
      errorRate.add(1);
      sleep(1);
      return;
    }

    const project = JSON.parse(res.body);
    const createdId = project.id;

    sleep(0.5);

    // 4. Consulta projeto criado
    res = http.get(`${API_URL}/projects/${createdId}`);
    check(res, {
      'get project success': (r) => r.status === 200,
      'correct project title': (r) => JSON.parse(r.body).title.includes('Projeto Teste'),
    }) || errorRate.add(1);

    sleep(0.5);

    // 5. Adiciona passo ao projeto
    const stepData = JSON.stringify({
      title: 'Passo 1 - Preparação',
      description: 'Preparar materiais e ferramentas',
      estimatedMinutes: 30,
      order: 1,
    });

    res = http.post(`${API_URL}/projects/${createdId}/steps`, stepData, { headers });
    check(res, {
      'add step success': (r) => r.status === 201,
    }) || errorRate.add(1);

    sleep(0.5);

    // 6. Busca projetos por categoria
    res = http.get(`${API_URL}/projects?category=Marcenaria&limit=5`);
    check(res, {
      'filter by category success': (r) => r.status === 200,
    }) || errorRate.add(1);

    sleep(1);
  });
}

// Teste de pico (Spike Testing)
export function spikeTest() {
  export let options = {
    stages: [
      { duration: '1m', target: 500 },  // Pico rápido
      { duration: '1m', target: 500 },  // Mantém pico
      { duration: '1m', target: 50 },   // Retorna ao normal
    ],
    thresholds: {
      http_req_duration: ['p(99)<5000'], // 99% < 5s durante pico
    },
  };

  // Executa requisições simples durante pico
  export default function () {
    const responses = http.batch([
      ['GET', `${BASE_URL}`],
      ['GET', `${API_URL}/projects`],
      ['GET', `${API_URL}/categories`],
    ]);

    check(responses[0], {
      'homepage during spike': (r) => r.status === 200,
    }) || errorRate.add(1);
  }
}

// Teste de resistência (Soak Testing)
export function soakTest() {
  export let options = {
    stages: [
      { duration: '30m', target: 100 },  // Carga sustentada por 30min
    ],
    thresholds: {
      http_req_duration: ['p(95)<3000'], // Performance estável
      'http_req_failed': ['rate<0.02'],  // Falhas < 2%
    },
  };

  export default function () {
    // Ciclo de operações variadas
    const operations = [
      () => http.get(BASE_URL),
      () => http.get(`${API_URL}/projects?limit=5`),
      () => http.get(`${API_URL}/projects?category=Marcenaria`),
    ];

    const op = operations[__ITER % operations.length];
    const res = op();

    check(res, {
      'soak test success': (r) => r.status === 200,
    }) || errorRate.add(1);

    sleep(Math.random

### [Sessão Paralela: Tech Writer]
# DIYAPP Evolution - V11 Core - Documentação de APIs e UI

## Estrutura do Projeto

```
diyapp-v11-core/
├── docs/
│   ├── api/
│   │   ├── openapi.yaml
│   │   ├── authentication.md
│   │   └── migration-guides/
│   ├── ui/
│   │   ├── component-guide.md
│   │   ├── dashboard-tutorial.md
│   │   └── troubleshooting.md
│   └── internal/
│       ├── adr-template.md
│       └── knowledge-base.md
├── public/
│   ├── index.html
│   ├── api-docs.html
│   └── ui-guide.html
├── src/
│   └── api/
│       └── docs-generator.js
└── package.json
```

## 1. Documentação OpenAPI/Swagger

### `docs/api/openapi.yaml`

```yaml
openapi: 3.0.3
info:
  title: DIYAPP Evolution V11 Core API
  description: |
    API principal do sistema DIYAPP Evolution V11.
    Sistema autônomo de fábrica de software com múltiplos agentes.
  version: 11.0.0
  contact:
    name: Squad Autônoma DIYAPP
    email: devops@diyapp.io
  license:
    name: MIT
    url: https://opensource.org/licenses/MIT

servers:
  - url: https://api.diyapp.io/v11
    description: Produção
  - url: https://staging-api.diyapp.io/v11
    description: Staging
  - url: http://localhost:3000/v11
    description: Desenvolvimento local

tags:
  - name: Authentication
    description: Autenticação e autorização
  - name: Projects
    description: Gerenciamento de projetos
  - name: Agents
    description: Controle de agentes autônomos
  - name: Monitoring
    description: Monitoramento e métricas
  - name: Documentation
    description: Geração e gestão de documentação

paths:
  /auth/login:
    post:
      tags:
        - Authentication
      summary: Autenticar usuário
      description: Realiza login e retorna token JWT
      requestBody:
        required: true
        content:
          application/json:
            schema:
              $ref: '#/components/schemas/LoginRequest'
      responses:
        '200':
          description: Login bem-sucedido
          content:
            application/json:
              schema:
                $ref: '#/components/schemas/LoginResponse'
        '401':
          description: Credenciais inválidas
          content:
            application/json:
              schema:
                $ref: '#/components/schemas/Error'
        '429':
          description: Muitas tentativas de login
          content:
            application/json:
              schema:
                $ref: '#/components/schemas/Error'

  /auth/refresh:
    post:
      tags:
        - Authentication
      summary: Refresh token
      description: Renova token de acesso usando refresh token
      security:
        - BearerAuth: []
      responses:
        '200':
          description: Token renovado
          content:
            application/json:
              schema:
                $ref: '#/components/schemas/RefreshResponse'
        '401':
          description: Token inválido ou expirado

  /projects:
    get:
      tags:
        - Projects
      summary: Listar projetos
      description: Retorna lista paginada de projetos
      security:
        - BearerAuth: []
      parameters:
        - in: query
          name: page
          schema:
            type: integer
            minimum: 1
            default: 1
          description: Número da página
        - in: query
          name: limit
          schema:
            type: integer
            minimum: 1
            maximum: 100
            default: 20
          description: Itens por página
        - in: query
          name: status
          schema:
            type: string
            enum: [active, archived, draft]
          description: Filtrar por status
      responses:
        '200':
          description: Lista de projetos
          content:
            application/json:
              schema:
                $ref: '#/components/schemas/ProjectList'
        '401':
          description: Não autorizado

    post:
      tags:
        - Projects
      summary: Criar novo projeto
      description: Cria um novo projeto na fábrica de software
      security:
        - BearerAuth: []
      requestBody:
        required: true
        content:
          application/json:
            schema:
              $ref: '#/components/schemas/CreateProjectRequest'
      responses:
        '201':
          description: Projeto criado
          content:
            application/json:
              schema:
                $ref: '#/components/schemas/Project'
        '400':
          description: Dados inválidos
        '401':
          description: Não autorizado

  /projects/{id}:
    get:
      tags:
        - Projects
      summary: Buscar projeto por ID
      description: Retorna detalhes completos de um projeto
      security:
        - BearerAuth: []
      parameters:
        - in: path
          name: id
          required: true
          schema:
            type: string
            format: uuid
          description: ID do projeto
      responses:
        '200':
          description: Detalhes do projeto
          content:
            application/json:
              schema:
                $ref: '#/components/schemas/Project'
        '404':
          description: Projeto não encontrado

    put:
      tags:
        - Projects
      summary: Atualizar projeto
      description: Atualiza informações de um projeto existente
      security:
        - BearerAuth: []
      parameters:
        - in: path
          name: id
          required: true
          schema:
            type: string
            format: uuid
          description: ID do projeto
      requestBody:
        required: true
        content:
          application/json:
            schema:
              $ref: '#/components/schemas/UpdateProjectRequest'
      responses:
        '200':
          description: Projeto atualizado
          content:
            application/json:
              schema:
                $ref: '#/components/schemas/Project'
        '404':
          description: Projeto não encontrado

    delete:
      tags:
        - Projects
      summary: Excluir projeto
      description: Exclui um projeto (soft delete)
      security:
        - BearerAuth: []
      parameters:
        - in: path
          name: id
          required: true
          schema:
            type: string
            format: uuid
          description: ID do projeto
      responses:
        '204':
          description: Projeto excluído
        '404':
          description: Projeto não encontrado

  /agents:
    get:
      tags:
        - Agents
      summary: Listar agentes
      description: Retorna status de todos os agentes autônomos
      security:
        - BearerAuth: []
      responses:
        '200':
          description: Lista de agentes
          content:
            application/json:
              schema:
                type: array
                items:
                  $ref: '#/components/schemas/AgentStatus'

  /agents/{agentId}/restart:
    post:
      tags:
        - Agents
      summary: Reiniciar agente
      description: Reinicia um agente específico
      security:
        - BearerAuth: []
      parameters:
        - in: path
          name: agentId
          required: true
          schema:
            type: string
            enum: [tech-writer, dev-backend, dev-frontend, sre, product-owner, tech-lead, innovation]
          description: ID do agente
      responses:
        '200':
          description: Agente reiniciado
          content:
            application/json:
              schema:
                $ref: '#/components/schemas/AgentStatus'
        '404':
          description: Agente não encontrado

  /monitoring/metrics:
    get:
      tags:
        - Monitoring
      summary: Obter métricas
      description: Retorna métricas do sistema em tempo real
      security:
        - BearerAuth: []
      responses:
        '200':
          description: Métricas do sistema
          content:
            application/json:
              schema:
                $ref: '#/components/schemas/Metrics'

  /docs/generate:
    post:
      tags:
        - Documentation
      summary: Gerar documentação
      description: Gera documentação automática para um projeto
      security:
        - BearerAuth: []
      requestBody:
        required: true
        content:
          application/json:
            schema:
              $ref: '#/components/schemas/GenerateDocsRequest'
      responses:
        '202':
          description: Documentação em processamento
          content:
            application/json:
              schema:
                $ref: '#/components/schemas/AsyncJob'

components:
  securitySchemes:
    BearerAuth:
      type: http
      scheme: bearer
      bearerFormat: JWT

  schemas:
    LoginRequest:
      type: object
      required:
        - email
        - password
      properties:
        email:
          type: string
          format: email
          example: user@diyapp.io
        password:
          type: string
          format: password
          example: "********"

    LoginResponse:
      type: object
      properties:
        accessToken:
          type: string
          description: Token JWT para autenticação
          example: "eyJhbGciOiJIUzI1NiIsInR5cCI6IkpXVCJ9..."
        refreshToken:
          type: string
          description: Token para renovar acesso
          example: "eyJhbGciOiJIUzI1NiIsInR5cCI6IkpXVCJ9..."
        expiresIn:
          type: integer
          description: Tempo de expiração em segundos
          example: 3600
        user:
          $ref: '#/components/schemas/User'

    RefreshResponse:
      type: object
      properties:
        accessToken:
          type: string
          example: "eyJhbGciOiJIUzI1NiIsInR5cCI6IkpXVCJ9..."
        expiresIn:
          type: integer
          example: 3600

    User:
      type: object
      properties:
        id:
          type: string
          format: uuid
        email:
          type: string
          format: email
        name:
          type: string
        role:
          type: string
          enum: [admin, developer, viewer]
        createdAt:
          type: string
          format: date-time

    CreateProjectRequest:
      type: object
      required:
        - name
        - template
      properties:
        name:
          type: string
          description: Nome do projeto
          example: "E-commerce Platform"
        description:
          type: string
          description: Descrição do projeto
          example: "Plataforma de e-commerce com múltiplos vendedores"
        template:
          type: string
          enum: [web-app, mobile-app, api-service, full-stack]
          description: Template inicial
        features:
          type: array
          items:
            type: string
          example: ["authentication", "payment", "inventory"]

    UpdateProjectRequest:
      type: object
      properties:
        name:
          type: string
        description:
          type: string
        status:
          type: string
          enum: [active, archived, draft]

    Project:
      type: object
      properties:
        id:
          type: string
          format: uuid
        name:
          type: string
        description:
          type: string
        status:
          type: string
          enum: [active, archived, draft]
        template:
          type: string
        features:
          type: array
          items:
            type: string
        createdAt:
          type: string
          format: date-time
        updatedAt:
          type: string
          format: date-time
        createdBy:
          $ref: '#/components/schemas/User'

    ProjectList:
      type: object
      properties:
        items:
          type: array
          items:
            $ref: '#/components/schemas/Project'
        total:
          type: integer
        page:
          type: integer
        limit:
          type: integer
        totalPages:
          type: integer

    AgentStatus:
      type: object
      properties:
        id:
          type: string
        name:
          type: string
        status:
          type: string
          enum: [running, stopped, error, starting]
        lastHeartbeat:
          type: string
          format: date-time
        cpuUsage:
          type: number
          format: float
        memoryUsage:
          type: number
          format: float

    Metrics:
      type: object
      properties:
        timestamp:
          type: string
          format: date-time
        system:
          $ref: '#/components/schemas/SystemMetrics'
        agents:
          type: array
          items:
            $ref: '#/components/schemas/AgentMetrics'
        projects:
          $ref: '#/components/schemas/ProjectMetrics'

    SystemMetrics:
      type: object
      properties:
        cpu:
          type: number
          format: float
        memory:
          type: number
          format: float
        disk:
          type: number
          format: float
        uptime:
          type: integer

    AgentMetrics:
      type: object
      properties:
        agentId:
          type: string
        requests:
          type: integer
        errors:
          type: integer
        avgResponseTime:
          type: number
          format: float

    ProjectMetrics:
      type: object
      properties:
        total:
          type: integer
        active:
          type: integer
        archived:
          type: integer

    GenerateDocsRequest:
      type: object
      required:
        - projectId
        - docType
      properties:
        projectId:
          type: string
          format: uuid
        docType:
          type: string
          enum: [api, ui, architecture, all]
        format:
          type: string
          enum: [html, pdf, markdown]
          default: html

    AsyncJob:
      type: object
      properties:
        jobId:
          type: string
          format: uuid
        status:
          type: string
          enum: [pending, processing, completed, failed]
        message:
          type: string
        estimatedCompletion:
          type: string
          format: date-time

    Error:
      type: object
      properties:
        error:
          type: string
        message:
          type: string
        code:
          type: integer
        timestamp:
          type: string
          format: date-time
        requestId:
          type: string
```

### `docs/api/authentication.md`

```markdown
# Guia de Autenticação - DIYAPP V11 API

## Visão Geral
A API DIYAPP V11 usa autenticação baseada em JWT (JSON Web Tokens). Todos os endpoints, exceto `/auth/login`, requerem um token de acesso válido.

## Fluxo de Autenticação

### 1. Obter Token de Acesso
```http
POST /auth/login
Content-Type: application/json

{
  "email": "seu-email@diyapp.io",
  "password": "sua-senha"
}
```

**Resposta de Sucesso:**
```json
{
  "accessToken": "eyJhbGciOiJIUzI1NiIsInR5cCI6IkpXVCJ9...",
  "refreshToken": "eyJhbGciOiJIUzI1NiIsInR5cCI6IkpXVCJ9...",
  "expiresIn": 3600,
  "user": {
    "id": "uuid",
    "email": "seu-email@diyapp.io",
    "name": "Seu Nome",
    "role": "developer"
  }
}
```

### 2. Usar Token em Requisições
Inclua o token no header `Authorization`:
```http
GET /projects
Authorization: Bearer eyJhbGciOiJIUzI1NiIsInR5cCI6IkpXVCJ9...
```

### 3. Renovar Token (quando expirar)
```http
POST /auth/refresh
Authorization: Bearer eyJhbGciOiJIUzI1NiIsInR5cCI6IkpXVCJ9...
```

## Exemplos de Código

### JavaScript/Node.js
```javascript
const axios = require('axios');

class DIYAPPClient {
  constructor(baseURL = 'https://api.diyapp.io/v11') {
    this.client = axios.create({ baseURL });
    this.token = null;
  }

  async login(email, password) {
    const response = await this.client.post('/auth/login', {
      email,
      password
    });
    
    this.token = response.data.accessToken;
    this.client.defaults.headers.common['Authorization'] = `Bearer ${this.token}`;
    
    return response.data;
  }

  async getProjects(page = 1, limit = 20) {
    const response = await this.client.get('/projects', {
      params: { page, limit }
    });
    
    return response.data;
  }
}

// Uso
const client = new DIYAPPClient();
await client.login('email@exemplo.com', 'senha');
const projects = await client.getProjects();
```

### Python
```python
import requests

class DIYAPPClient:
    def __init__(self, base_url="https://api.diyapp.io/v11"):
        self.base_url = base_url
        self.session = requests.Session()
        self.token = None
    
    def login(self, email, password):
        response = self.session.post(
            f"{self.base_url}/auth/login",
            json={"email": email, "password": password}
        )
        response.raise_for_status()
        
        data = response.json()
        self.token = data["accessToken"]
        self.session.headers.update({
            "Authorization": f"Bearer {self.token}"
        })
        
        return data
    
    def get_projects(self, page=1, limit=20):
        response = self.session.get(
            f"{self.base_url}/projects",
